\DoxyCodeLine{1062   \textcolor{comment}{// The following logic is a bit complicated to decipher because we}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1063   \textcolor{comment}{// want to retain backwards compatible semantics:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1064   \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1065   \textcolor{comment}{// (a) When no `Runtime` domain is enabled, we stick to the default}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1066   \textcolor{comment}{//     maximum call stack size, but don't let V8 collect stack traces}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1067   \textcolor{comment}{//     for uncaught exceptions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1068   \textcolor{comment}{// (b) When `Runtime` is enabled for at least one front-\/end, we compute}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1069   \textcolor{comment}{//     the maximum of the requested maximum call stack sizes of all the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1070   \textcolor{comment}{//     front-\/ends whose `Runtime` domains are enabled (which might be 0),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1071   \textcolor{comment}{//     and ask V8 to collect stack traces for uncaught exceptions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1072   \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1073   \textcolor{comment}{// The latter allows performance test automation infrastructure to drive}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1074   \textcolor{comment}{// browser via `Runtime` domain while still minimizing the performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1075   \textcolor{comment}{// overhead of having the inspector attached -\/ see the relevant design}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1076   \textcolor{comment}{// document https://bit.ly/v8-\/cheaper-\/inspector-\/stack-\/traces for more}}
